GFL\u2019s target price to Rs 3,798, indicating an upside of 9.6%, highlighting the firm\u2019s battery materials business as a key driver. GFL is one of the few non-China integrated producers of LiPF6, a crucial battery ingredient. Plants for these materials have been commissioned, with commercial sales expected from Q4FY26.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;GFL\u2019s growth comes from high-margin fluoropolymers (63% of Q2FY26 revenue), fluorochemicals, and rising demand for R32 refrigerant. In&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/fundamentals/financials/169265/FLUOROCHEM/gujarat-fluorochemicals-ltd/\&quot; style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt; &lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#1155cc\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:underline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;-webkit-text-decoration-skip:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration-skip-ink:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Q2FY26&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;, revenue rose 2% YoY, mainly due to fluoropolymers and higher chloromethane prices. EBITDA margin improved by 525 bps to 30% as the company sold more higher-value grades of fluoropolymers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Some hurdles remain, including temporary volume impacts from US tariffs on certain fluoropolymers and the R125 refrigerant. Fluorochemical revenue slipped 15% due to lower R-22 sales, a widely used refrigerant being phased out globally. The battery chemicals business is still pre-revenue and posted an EBITDA loss of Rs 17 crore.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;CEO Bir Kapoor expects the battery chemicals business to break even in FY27. He says, \u201cFY28 should be a major scale-up year as new capacity comes online and customers approve the products\u201d. the new units will be strategically placed near project sites to slash logistics costs. Two plants are planned for Gujarat and Karnataka; a third location is being scouted. The facilities will be funded internally, falling within the company\u2019s annual capital expenditure of Rs 500\u2013550 crore. These additions will expand the company\u2019s network to 18 factories, creating India&#x27;s largest smart wind manufacturing setup.\u00a0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; that a major deal had fallen through. Global private equity firm Advent International was in talks to acquire a controlling stake in the company for up to $1 billion, but negotiations reportedly collapsed due to disagreements over valuation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Advent had been the frontrunner to buy a 31% stake from the company&#x27;s US parent, Whirlpool Corporation, a move that would have triggered a mandatory takeover offer. The parent company, looking to pay down debt by restructuring its global assets, planned to reduce its 51% holding to roughly 20% and raise between $550 million and $600 million. However, the deal stalled as Advent &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/posts/5437283/advent-s-1-bn-deal-talks-for-whirlpool-india-collapse-due-to-disagreements\&quot; the acquisition of a 50% stake in Nexus Holdco FZCO for $55 million (approximately Rs 495.7 crore). The company will carry out this acquisition through its subsidiary, Lloyds Global Resources FZCO.\u00a0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Nexus holds significant stakes in Surya Mines SARL and eight other companies in the Democratic Republic of Congo. These companies collectively control various mining concessions, including copper, cobalt, lead, and zinc, as well as a copper processing plant in the country.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;The company also &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/posts/5441011/lloyds-metals-and-energy-ltd-512455-announcement-under-regulation-30-lodr-press-release-media-release\&quot; style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#1155cc\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:underline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;-webkit-text-decoration-skip:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration-skip-ink:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;signed&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt; a memorandum of understanding (MoU) with Tata Steel to collaborate on raw material mining, logistics, pellet, and steel-making. The partnership will focus on greenfield steel-making projects, iron ore mining, slurry pipeline infrastructure, pellet-making in iron ore-rich Indian states, and exporting low-carbon iron &amp; steel products. Initially, they will operate mining concessions and associated infrastructure to boost iron ore production in Gadchiroli, Maharashtra.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;In &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/fundamentals/financials/2582/LLOYDSME/lloyds-metals-energy-ltd/\&quot; Revenue also beat Forecaster estimates by 27.9%. Net profit jumped 90%, driven by the commercialisation of the slurry pipeline and improved fixed-cost management. However, the company\u2019s debt surged 75% to Rs 8,000 crore due to delays in capacity expansion in its arm, Thriveni Earthmovers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Following the results, Riyaz Shaikh, CFO of Lloyds Metals, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/posts/5419212/lloyds-metals-and-energy-ltd-512455-announcement-under-regulation-30-lodr-earnings-call-transcript\&quot; style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#1155cc\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:underline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;-webkit-text-decoration-skip:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration-skip-ink:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;noted&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;, \u201cWe have lowered our FY26 EBITDA guidance for Thriveni to ~Rs 2,100 crore from Rs 2,800 crore due to delayed capacity ramp-up, with confidence in catching up in H2.\u201d&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;FundsIndia &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/posts/5440808/empowering-indias-infrastructure\&quot; style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#1155cc\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:underline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;-webkit-text-decoration-skip:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration-skip-ink:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;maintains&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt; its \u2018Buy\u2019 call on Lloyds Metals, setting a target price of Rs 1,468 per share, a 14% upside. The brokerage believes the company is poised for long-term growth as its capacity expansions commercialise over the next 2-3 years. It expects Lloyds Metals\u2019 capex to rise to Rs 6,000-6,500 crore from FY27 onwards, supporting its shift from ore sales to an integrated pellet, direct-reduced iron, and steel model.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;\r\n\u00a0&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-d4922455-7fff-dd65-8388-7e768885e4f1\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:italic\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Trendlyne&#x27;s analysts identify stocks that are seeing interesting price movements, analyst calls, or new developments. These are not buy recommendations&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&quot;, &quot;pubDate&quot;: &quot;2025-12-12T10:53:55+00:00&quot;, &quot;source&quot;: &quot;Trendlyne&quot;, &quot;pdfUrl&quot;: null, &quot;videoUrl&quot;: null, &quot;embedvideoUrl&quot;: null, &quot;imageUrl&quot;: &quot;https://trendlyne-media-mumbai-new.s3.amazonaws.com/post-files/2025-12-12/None-b23ed12b1a7041c39132822136c5762f.webp&quot;, &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://trendlyne.com/posts/5443197/five-interesting-stocks-today-december-12-2025?tlsource=clientapp&quot;, &quot;pk&quot;: 5443197, &quot;share_count&quot;: 0, &quot;like_count&quot;: 0, &quot;liked_posts&quot;: false, &quot;get_embed_data&quot;: null, &quot;post_absolute_url&quot;: &quot;https://trendlyne.com/posts/5443197/five-interesting-stocks-today-december-12-2025&quot;}, {&quot;title&quot;: &quot;Five stocks to buy from analysts this week - December 11, 2025&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;1. Coforge:  Motilal Oswal maintains its \u2018Buy\u2019 call on this digital services provider, with a target price of Rs 3,000 per share, an upside of 63.7%. Analysts Abhishek Pathak and Keval Bhagat view Coforge as a strong mid-tier player, well-positioned to benefit from vendor consolidation and rising demand for cost-optimisation deals. Management highlighted increased client budgets for compliance and risk management due to tightening financial regulations, data protection &amp; privacy laws, and AI governance &amp; ethics. Analysts believe this offers Coforge a resilient, non-discretionary revenue stream. They add that AI-led legacy modernisation and cloud transformation are accelerating enterprise-wide automation. Analysts also note a pivot in the travel technology vertical (23% of revenue), with airlines expected to invest approximately $50 billion in modernisation over the next decade. Coforge\u2019s Aeronova.AI platform enhances its competitive standing in this segment. The company plans expansion into the West and Midwest of North America, focusing on hi-tech, retail, consumer packaged goods, and manufacturing verticals. Pathak and Bhagat see Coforge\u2019s strong executable order book and resilient client spending driving long-term growth. They expect a revenue CAGR of 30.2% and a net profit CAGR of 38.7% over FY26-28. 2. Healthcare Global Enterprises: Axis Direct retains its \u2018Buy\u2019 call on this healthcare services provider with a target price of Rs 850 per share, an upside of 20.1%. The company\u2019s stock price has shown weakness recently, falling 7.7% over the past month. Analyst Aman Goyal is positive on the stock, owing to strong growth in oncology, management\u2019s confidence in sustaining revenue and profitability, and Rs 290 crore in capex for FY27 expansion. Management anticipates 9-10% growth in patient volume and a 4-5% increase in average revenue per patient (ARPP). They expect deeper clinical specialisations, scaling key programs like bone marrow transplant and robotic surgery, better patient journeys, and stronger sales efforts to drive this growth. Analyst notes the company will benefit from improved operating leverage, a better case mix, and a shift from lower-yield institutional business, supporting management\u2019s EBITDA margin guidance of 21-22% over the next 4-5 years.  Goyal highlights that Healthcare Global\u2019s Rs 600-700 crore capex over the next 2-3 years will fund brownfield expansions and greenfield acquisitions in key markets. He expects the company to deliver a revenue CAGR of 15.7% and a net profit CAGR of 80.5% over FY26-28. 3. Union Bank of India:  Geojit BNP Paribas reiterates its \u2018Buy\u2019 call on this public sector bank, with a target price of Rs 188 per share, an upside of 25.1%. The bank\u2019s Q2FY26 net profit rose 3.3% sequentially to Rs 4,249.1 crore. Analyst Sheen G points to an 8.3% drop in gross slippages, along with improved credit underwriting and recovery, as key catalysts for net profit growth. The analyst notes that the bank improved its asset quality, with net non-performing assets falling 43 bps YoY to 0.6%, supported by strong provisioning. However, net interest income (NII) declined 2.6% due to slower loan growth and higher deposit costs. Net interest margin also contracted 23 basis points to 2.7%, reflecting deposit repricing and cautious lending in lower-yield segments.  Management expects to achieve 9-10% loan growth going forward, driven by an improving loan mix. Sheen highlights that the bank\u2019s 5% loan growth came from strong increases in the retail, agriculture, and MSME segments. The analyst projects a NII CAGR of 7.4% over FY26-27. 4. SRF:  ICICI Securities upgrades this chemical company to a \u2018Buy\u2019 rating, with a target price of Rs 3,450, an upside of 17.2%. Over the last six months, the stock has corrected by 4.8%. Analysts Sanjesh Jain and Mohit Mishra expect a broad recovery across SRF\u2019s chemicals portfolio and see a 15\u201320% upside to current revenue forecasts for refrigerant gases, supported by stronger volumes and stable global prices. Management reports strong demand for SRF\u2019s main gas product, R32 (a hydrofluorocarbon), even as the world transitions from older gases. They expect long-term demand to grow as new US rules mandate air conditioners to use newer gases like R454B, which contains R32. Growing data centres in the US and China also add demand. For its R134a gas product, which is used mainly in automobile air-conditioning, analysts cite strong domestic car sales and India\u2019s mandate for air-conditioned cabins in commercial vehicles as key demand drivers. Management also expects the speciality chemicals business to improve in the second half of FY26 with new product production.  Jain and Mishra believe SRF will benefit from steady demand, limited competition, and growth in the fluoropolymer market. They project stronger revenue and net profit led by refrigerant gases, and note that demand for hydrofluorocarbon gases remains favourable amid improving industry conditions. 5. Voltamp Transformers:  Emkay maintains its \u2018Buy\u2019 rating on this transformer manufacturer with a target price of Rs 10,000, an upside of 25.3%. Its share price has fallen 10.9% over the last six months and 29.4% over the past year. Analysts Ashwani Sharma and Abhishek Taparia note that the company holds about a 15% share in the industrial transformer market, supported by a strong presence among private-sector clients. With nearly 85% of its revenue coming from this segment, they view the company\u2019s customer base as both stable and well diversified.  Management reports strong inquiries from industrial customers and power utilities as grid expansion accelerates. Order inflows have been robust, growing 37% in FY24, 12% in FY25, and another 37% in the first half of FY26. Demand comes from sectors like metals, mining, infrastructure, and renewable energy. Voltamp currently operates at full capacity of 14,000 megavolt ampere (MVA) and adds another 6,000 MVA in Vadodara by FY27 to support future growth.   Sharma and Taparia see good opportunities in solar, railways, EV charging, and data centres. While competition might soften margins, they maintain a positive long-term view, backed by strong demand, a Rs 1,400 crore order book, and planned expansion. They expect strong revenue growth but slightly reduced margin expectations due to new industry capacity and potential price pressure.   Note: These recommendations are from various analysts and are not recommendations by Trendlyne. The bank\u2019s &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://trendlyne.com/fundamentals/financials/1447/UNIONBANK/union-bank-of-india/\&quot; style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#1155cc\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:underline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;-webkit-text-decoration-skip:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration-skip-ink:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Q2FY26&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt; net profit rose 3.3% sequentially to Rs 4,249.1 crore. Analyst Sheen G points to an 8.3% drop in gross slippages, along with improved credit underwriting and recovery, as key catalysts for net profit growth.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-8dc962f2-7fff-e502-cfc9-d2650514d9c8\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;The analyst notes that the bank improved its asset quality, with net non-performing assets falling 43 bps YoY to 0.6%, supported by strong provisioning. However, net interest income (NII) declined 2.6% due to slower loan growth and higher deposit costs. Net interest margin also contracted 23 basis points to 2.7%, reflecting deposit repricing and cautious lending in lower-yield segments.\u00a0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-8dc962f2-7fff-e502-cfc9-d2650514d9c8\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Management expects to achieve 9-10% loan growth going forward, driven by an improving loan mix. Sheen highlights that the bank\u2019s 5% loan growth came from strong increases in the retail, agriculture, and MSME segments. The analyst projects a NII CAGR of 7.4% over FY26-27.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;h3 dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; company to a \u2018Buy\u2019 rating, with a target price of Rs 3,450, an upside of 17.2%. Over the last six months, the stock has corrected by 4.8%. Analysts Sanjesh Jain and Mohit Mishra expect a broad recovery across SRF\u2019s chemicals portfolio and see a 15\u201320% upside to current revenue forecasts for refrigerant gases, supported by stronger volumes and stable global prices.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-8dc962f2-7fff-e502-cfc9-d2650514d9c8\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Management reports strong demand for SRF\u2019s main gas product, R32 (a hydrofluorocarbon), even as the world transitions from older gases. They expect long-term demand to grow as new US rules mandate air conditioners to use newer gases like R454B, which contains R32. Growing data centres in the US and China also add demand. For its R134a gas product, which is used mainly in automobile air-conditioning, analysts cite strong domestic car sales and India\u2019s mandate for air-conditioned cabins in commercial vehicles as key demand drivers. Management also expects the speciality chemicals business to improve in the second half of FY26 with new product production.\u00a0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-8dc962f2-7fff-e502-cfc9-d2650514d9c8\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Jain and Mishra believe SRF will benefit from steady demand, limited competition, and growth in the fluoropolymer market. manufacturer with a target price of Rs 10,000, an upside of 25.3%. Its share price has fallen 10.9% over the last six months and 29.4% over the past year. Analysts Ashwani Sharma and Abhishek Taparia note that the company holds about a 15% share in the industrial transformer market, supported by a strong presence among private-sector clients. With nearly 85% of its revenue coming from this segment, they view the company\u2019s customer base as both stable and well diversified.\u00a0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-8dc962f2-7fff-e502-cfc9-d2650514d9c8\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Management reports strong inquiries from industrial customers and power utilities as grid expansion accelerates. Order inflows have been robust, growing 37% in FY24, 12% in FY25, and another 37% in the first half of FY26. Demand comes from sectors like metals, mining, infrastructure, and renewable energy. Voltamp currently operates at full capacity of 14,000 megavolt ampere (MVA) and adds another 6,000 MVA in Vadodara by FY27 to support future growth. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;\r\n&lt;br /&gt;\r\n&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#000000\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Sharma and Taparia see good opportunities in solar, railways, EV charging, and data centres. While competition might soften margins, they maintain a positive long-term view, backed by strong demand, a Rs 1,400 crore order book, and planned expansion. They expect strong revenue growth but slightly reduced margin expectations due to new industry capacity and potential price pressure.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p&gt;\u00a0&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot; style=\&quot;text-align:justify; margin-top:13px; margin-bottom:13px\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;line-height:1.38\&quot;&gt;&lt;b id=\&quot;docs-internal-guid-8dc962f2-7fff-e502-cfc9-d2650514d9c8\&quot; style=\&quot;font-weight:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-size:11pt\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-family:Arial,sans-serif\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;color:#202124\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-weight:400\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-style:italic\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;font-variant:normal\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;text-decoration:none\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;vertical-align:baseline\&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap\&quot;&gt;Note: These recommendations are from various analysts and are not recommendations by Trendlyne.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p dir=\&quot;ltr\&quot;
